    const stillExists = this.sessionManager.getSession(sessionDbId);\n   285→                if (stillExists && !stillExists.generatorPromise) {\n   286→      // No pending work - abort to kill the child process\n   291→              session.abortController.abort();\n   292→              // Reset restart counter on successful completion\n   293→              session.consecutiveRestarts = 0;\n   294→              logger.debug('SESSION', 'Aborted controller after natural completion', {\n   295→                sessionId: sessionDbId\n   296→              });\n   297→            }\n   298→          } catch (e) {\n   299→            // Ignore errors during recovery check, but still abort to prevent leaks\n   300→            logger.debug('SESSION', 'Error during recovery check, aborting to prevent leaks', { sessionId: sessionDbId, error: e instanceof Error ? e.message : String(e) });\n   301→            session.abortController.abort();\n   302→          }\n   303→        }\n   304→        // NOTE: We do NOT delete the session here anymore.\n   305→        // The generator waits for events, so if it exited, it's either aborted or crashed.\n   306→        // Idle sessions stay in memory (ActiveSession is small) to listen for future events.\n   307→      });\n   308→  }\n   309→\n   310→  setupRoutes(app: express.Application): void {\n Let me write the proposal.\n\n---\n\n# Privacy Mode Toggle: Proposal\n\n## Overview\n\nThe goal is a global `CLAUDE_MEM_PRIVACY_MODE` setting that, when set to `'true'`, causes the observer to silently skip all observation and summary storage entirely — not just strip `<private>` tags, but produce no database writes at all. Context injection (SessionStart / reading from the DB) continues to work normally. This is a \"pause recording\" capability, not a full plugin disable.\n\n---\n\n## What Happens Today (Storage Pipeline)\n\nUnderstanding what needs to be gated is critical before proposing where to add the check.\n\n**Flow:**\n\n```\nPostToolUse/Stop hook\n  → hook handler (observation.ts / summarize.ts)\n    → POST /api/sessions/observations or /api/sessions/summarize (worker)\n      → handleObservationsByClaudeId / handleSummarizeByClaudeId\n        → sessionManager.queueObservation / queueSummarize\n          → ensureGeneratorRunning → SDKAgent / GeminiAgent / OpenRouterAgent\n            → processAgentResponse → sessionStore.storeObservations / storeSummary\n              → ChromaSync (async)\n              → SSE broadcast (async)\n```\n\n**Session init also writes to the DB:**\n\n```\nUserPromptSubmit hook\n  → session-init.ts\n    → POST /api/sessions/init\n      → handleSessionInitByClaudeId\n        → store.createSDKSession (idempotent INSERT OR IGNORE on sessions table)\n        → store.saveUserPrompt (writes to user_prompts table)\n```\n\n**What privacy mode needs to suppress:**\n1. The `saveUserPrompt` call in `handleSessionInitByClaudeId`\n2. The `queueObservation` call in `handleObservationsByClaudeId` (and therefore the downstream `storeObservations` + `storeSummary`)\n3. The `queueSummarize` call in `handleSummarizeByClaudeId`\n4. `createSDKSession` is idempotent and only writes a skeleton row — it can be left alone since it produces no meaningful data (just an ID reference). The session row has no private content.\n\nThe SDK agent should not be started at all in privacy mode (no generator spawn), since there is nothing to process.\n\n---\n\n## Proposed Approach\n\n### 1. Toggle Mechanism: `CLAUDE_MEM_PRIVACY_MODE` Setting\n\n**Where:** `src/shared/SettingsDefaultsManager.ts`\n\nAdd a new entry to the `SettingsDefaults` interface and `DEFAULTS` object:\n\n```typescript\n// In SettingsDefaults interface\nCLAUDE_MEM_PRIVACY_MODE: string;  // 'true' | 'false' — skip all observation storage when enabled\n\n// In DEFAULTS\nCLAUDE_MEM_PRIVACY_MODE: 'false',\n```\n\nThis follows the exact same pattern as every other boolean feature toggle already in the system (`CLAUDE_MEM_FOLDER_CLAUDEMD_ENABLED`, `CLAUDE_MEM_CONTEXT_SHOW_LAST_SUMMARY`, etc.). The string `'true'`/`'false'` format is consistent with all existing boolean settings in this codebase.\n\n---\n\n### 2. Files to Modify\n\n#### A. `src/shared/SettingsDefaultsManager.ts`\n\nAdd the interface field and default value as described above. This is the single source of truth for all settings.\n\n#### B. `src/services/worker/http/routes/SessionRoutes.ts`\n\nThis is where the actual gating should live — at the **worker's HTTP boundary**, not in the hooks. Three locations within this file:\n\n**In `handleSessionInitByClaudeId` (~line 759):** Skip `saveUserPrompt` when privacy mode is enabled. The `createSDKSession` call can remain (it only writes a skeleton row for FK purposes). The `contextInjected` check also remains intact since context reading is unaffected.\n\n```typescript\n// After Step 3 (strip privacy tags), before Step 5 (save user prompt):\nconst privacyModeEnabled = settings.CLAUDE_MEM_PRIVACY_MODE === 'true';\nif (privacyModeEnabled) {\n  logger.debug('SESSION', 'Privacy mode enabled, skipping user prompt storage', {\n    sessionId: sessionDbId,\n    promptNumber\n  });\n  res.json({ sessionDbId, promptNumber, skipped: true, reason: 'privacy_mode' });\n  return;\n}\n```\n\n**In `handleObservationsByClaudeId` (~line 498):** Skip queueing observations when privacy mode is enabled. Load settings (already loaded for `SKIP_TOOLS`) and add a check after the skip tools check:\n\n```typescript\nconst settings = SettingsDefaultsManager.loadFromFile(USER_SETTINGS_PATH);\nif (settings.CLAUDE_MEM_PRIVACY_MODE === 'true') {\n  logger.debug('SESSION', 'Privacy mode enabled, skipping observation', { tool_name });\n  res.json({ status: 'skipped', reason: 'privacy_mode' });\n  return;\n}\n```\n\n**In `handleSummarizeByClaudeId` (~line 596):** Skip queueing the summarize request:\n\n```typescript\nconst settings = SettingsDefaultsManager.loadFromFile(USER_SETTINGS_PATH);\nif (settings.CLAUDE_MEM_PRIVACY_MODE === 'true') {\n  logger.debug('SESSION', 'Privacy mode enabled, skipping summarize', { contentSessionId });\n  res.json({ status: 'skipped', reason: 'privacy_mode' });\n  return;\n}\n```\n\nNote: `settings` is already loaded in `handleObservationsByClaudeId` for `SKIP_TOOLS`. The privacy mode check should be added right after that load to avoid a second read.\n\n#### C. `src/services/worker/http/routes/SettingsRoutes.ts`\n\nAdd `CLAUDE_MEM_PRIVACY_MODE` to the `settingKeys` array in `handleUpdateSettings` (line ~87) so it can be toggled via the API:\n\n```typescript\n'CLAUDE_MEM_PRIVACY_MODE',\n```\n\nAlso add it to the boolean validation list in `validateSettings`:\n\n```typescript\nconst booleanSettings = [\n  // ... existing entries ...\n  'CLAUDE_MEM_PRIVACY_MODE',\n];\n```\n\n#### D. `src/ui/viewer/constants/settings.ts`\n\nAdd to `DEFAULT_SETTINGS`:\n\n```typescript\nCLAUDE_MEM_PRIVACY_MODE: 'false',\n```\n\n---\n\n### 3. Integration with the Existing Hook Lifecycle\n\nThe check lives **entirely in the worker** (SessionRoutes), not in the hook handlers. This is the correct layer because:\n\n- The hooks are thin — they already do the `isProjectExcluded` check at hook layer for excluded projects, but for privacy mode (a global toggle rather than path-based filter) the worker layer is cleaner\n- `handleObservationsByClaudeId` already loads settings for `SKIP_TOOLS`, so loading them once and checking privacy mode is zero additional I/O\n- The worker is the canonical gatekeeper for \"should this data be stored\" — see `PrivacyCheckValidator` already living there\n\nThe full lifecycle with privacy mode enabled:\n\n```\nSessionStart  → context handler (still runs, reads from DB — UNAFFECTED)\nUserPromptSubmit → session-init.ts → /api/sessions/init\n    → createSDKSession (skeleton row only, no user data)\n    → [SKIPPED: saveUserPrompt] → returns { skipped: true, reason: 'privacy_mode' }\n    → session-init.ts: initResult.skipped = true\n    → hook returns { continue: true } (Claude is not blocked)\n\nPostToolUse → observation.ts → /api/sessions/observations\n    → [SKIPPED] → returns { status: 'skipped', reason: 'privacy_mode' }\n    → hook returns gracefully\n\nStop (Summary) → summarize.ts → /api/sessions/summarize\n    → [SKIPPED] → returns { status: 'skipped', reason: 'privacy_mode' }\n    → hook returns gracefully\n\nStop (SessionComplete) → session-complete.ts → /api/sessions/complete\n    → completionHandler.completeByDbId (removes from active sessions map)\n    → UNAFFECTED — this is cleanup, not storage\n```\n\nContext injection at `SessionStart` continues to provide past memories. Only new writes are suppressed.\n\n---\n\n### 4. API Endpoint for Toggle\n\nOnce `CLAUDE_MEM_PRIVACY_MODE` is in the settings schema, the existing `POST /api/settings` endpoint handles it automatically. No new endpoint is needed.\n\nThe Viewer UI would need a toggle added to `ContextSettingsModal.tsx` — a simple boolean toggle following the existing `CLAUDE_MEM_CONTEXT_SHOW_LAST_SUMMARY` pattern.\n\n---\n\n### 5. Alternative Considered: Hook-Layer Check\n\nAn alternative is to add the check in `observation.ts` and `session-init.ts` at the hook layer (following the `isProjectExcluded` pattern). This would be slightly faster (avoids the HTTP round-trip entirely) and is already consistent with how excluded projects work.\n\nThe trade-off: hook-layer checks make it easier to accidentally skip loading settings (they already load settings twice today — once in `session-init.ts` and once in `observation.ts`). The worker-layer approach centralizes all storage decisions in one place, which is more maintainable and less likely to develop gaps (e.g., the `file-edit` handler would also need its own check at the hook layer).\n\n**Recommendation:** Do it at the **worker layer** (SessionRoutes) because:\n- Every storage path flows through SessionRoutes\n- The `file-edit` handler in `fileEditHandler.ts` also routes to `/api/sessions/observations` — the worker check covers it for free without touching `file-edit.ts`\n- The worker already owns privacy semantics (`PrivacyCheckValidator`)\n\n---\n\n### 6. Concerns and Trade-offs\n\n**Concern 1: Settings are read on every request (no in-memory cache)**\n`SettingsDefaultsManager.loadFromFile` reads and parses `settings.json` on every call. This is fine for the infrequent sessions/init and sessions/summarize endpoints, but `sessions/observations` fires on every tool use. The current codebase already does this for `SKIP_TOOLS` on every observation, so there is no regression introduced. If it ever becomes a bottleneck, the pattern used elsewhere (loading once and caching) can be applied — but YAGNI says don't do it until measured.\n\n**Concern 2: Skeleton session rows still written**\nWhen privacy mode is on, `createSDKSession` still runs in `handleObservationsByClaudeId` and `handleSessionInitByClaudeId`. This writes a minimal row (session ID, empty project, empty prompt) to the sessions table. This is intentional — these rows contain no meaningful user data and are required for FK integrity if a future mode switch tries to backfill observations into the same session. If that is undesirable, `createSDKSession` can also be skipped by returning early before it is called.\n\n**Concern 3: No visual indicator in the terminal output**\nWhen privacy mode is enabled, the `user-message` handler still runs at `SessionStart` and shows the \"Claude-Mem Context Loaded\" banner. This could mislead the user into thinking observations are being stored. The banner in `user-message.ts` should ideally show a \"privacy mode: recording paused\" notice. This is a small addition to `user-message.ts`: load settings, check `CLAUDE_MEM_PRIVACY_MODE`, and append a notice to the stderr output.\n\n**Concern 4: Context injection still works — is that correct?**\nYes. Privacy mode is \"pause recording\", not \"disable memory\". The user still benefits from past sessions. If the intent were to also hide past memories from the context, that would be a separate \"disable memory context\" setting, not \"privacy mode\". The name \"privacy mode\" clearly communicates that new data is not being stored.\n\n**Concern 5: No session-scoped privacy mode**\nThis is a global toggle. There is no way to say \"only pause recording for this project\" — that's what `CLAUDE_MEM_EXCLUDED_PROJECTS` already handles. Privacy mode is intentionally simpler: flip one switch to pause everything everywhere. Combining both approaches would create confusion about precedence.\n\n**Concern 6: The SDK agent is never spawned**\nWhen observations are skipped before `queueObservation`, `ensureGeneratorRunning` is never called. The SDK agent is never spawned. This is desirable — no unnecessary AI processing costs when nothing will be stored.\n\n---\n\n## Summary of Files to Modify\n\n| File | Change |\n|---|---|\n| `src/shared/SettingsDefaultsManager.ts` | Add `CLAUDE_MEM_PRIVACY_MODE: string` to interface and defaults |\n| `src/services/worker/http/routes/SessionRoutes.ts` | Check privacy mode in 3 handlers: `handleSessionInitByClaudeId`, `handleObservationsByClaudeId`, `handleSummarizeByClaudeId` |\n| `src/services/worker/http/routes/SettingsRoutes.ts` | Add `CLAUDE_MEM_PRIVACY_MODE` to `settingKeys` array and `booleanSettings` validation list |\n| `src/ui/viewer/constants/settings.ts` | Add `CLAUDE_MEM_PRIVACY_MODE: 'false'` to `DEFAULT_SETTINGS` |\n| `src/cli/handlers/user-message.ts` | Optional: display \"recording paused\" notice in terminal banner when privacy mode is active |"}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1035,"cache_read_input_tokens":83817,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1035},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"}},"requestId":"req_011CYUR4q2K7qSowMFTV3JJq","type":"assistant","uuid":"11d70ebb-bc58-4d2b-af83-46018cb795dd","timestamp":"2026-02-25T07:46:55.656Z"}
